  // LMDA.device DEPRECATED, only for django compability
  LMDA.device = LMDA.device || {};
  LMDA.device.high_quality_image = function (imgSrc) {
    if (LMDA.device.is_high_quality_image) {
      return imgSrc.replace('img389x562', 'product')
      .replace('236x341', '389x562')
      .replace('46x66', '135x194');
    }
    return imgSrc;
  };

  function recalcClasses() {
    var width = root.clientWidth;
    var newSize = 'desktop';
    var newOrientation = (window.innerHeight > window.innerWidth) ? 'portrait' : 'landscape';
    if (width < 768) {
      newSize = 'phone';
    } else if (width < 992) {
      newSize = 'tablet';
    } else if (width > 1245) {
      newSize = 'wide';
    }
    if (size !== newSize) {
      root.classList.remove('html_' + size);
      root.classList.add('html_' + newSize);
      size = newSize;
      if (newSize === 'wide') {
        root.classList.add('widescreen');
        LMDA.isWidescreen = false;
      }
      LMDA.device.size = newSize;
    }
    if (currentOrientation !== newOrientation) {
      root.classList.remove('html_' + currentOrientation);
      root.classList.add('html_' + newOrientation);
      currentOrientation = newOrientation;
      LMDA.device.orientation = newOrientation;
    }
  }

  function throttleOnResize() {
    if (!resizeTimeout) {
      resizeTimeout = setTimeout(function () {
        resizeTimeout = null;
        recalcClasses();
      }, 300);
    }
  }

  (function () {
    var tcpInfo = "2643, 36101, 18472";
    if (tcpInfo) {
        var rtt = parseInt(tcpInfo.split(", ")[2]);
    }
    var speed = 'fast';
    var isRetina;
    var isMobile;

    if (rtt > 75000) {
      speed = 'slow';
    } else if (rtt > 25000) {
      speed = 'normal';
    }
    LMDA.device.network = speed;

    isMobile = size === 'phone' || size === 'tablet';
    isRetina = speed !== 'slow' && (
      (isMobile && window.devicePixelRatio >= 3) ||
      (!isMobile && window.devicePixelRatio >= 2)
    );

    if (isRetina) {
      root.classList.add('html_retina');
      LMDA.device.isRetina = true;
    }
    if ('ontouchstart' in document.documentElement) {
      root.classList.add('html_touch', 'touch');
      LMDA.isTouch = true;
    } else {
      LMDA.device.isTouch = false;
      root.classList.add('html_not-touch', 'not-touch');
    }

            var aoHiddenBlocks = document.querySelectorAll('.header__top-items .header__top-item[data-aoid]');
            var aoVisibleBlocks = document.querySelectorAll('.header__top-items .header__top-item[data-hideby-aoid]');

            if (aoHiddenBlocks && aoHiddenBlocks.length) {
              for (var i in aoHiddenBlocks) {
                if (aoHiddenBlocks[i] && typeof(aoHiddenBlocks[i]) == 'object') {
                  if (aoHiddenBlocks[i].getAttribute('data-aoid').search(aoId) > -1) {
                    aoHiddenBlocks[i].style.display = 'block';
                  }
                }
              }
            }

            if (aoVisibleBlocks && aoVisibleBlocks.length) {
              for (var i in aoVisibleBlocks) {
                if (aoVisibleBlocks[i] && typeof(aoVisibleBlocks[i]) == 'object') {
                  if (aoVisibleBlocks[i].getAttribute('data-hideby-aoid').search(aoId) > -1) {
                    aoVisibleBlocks[i].style.display = 'none';
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          </script>
